  | "a" -> "A"
  | "b" -> "B"
  | "c" -> "C"
  | "d" -> "D"
  | "e" -> "E"

  | "a" -> "A"
  | "b" -> "B"
  | "c" -> "C"
  | "d" -> "D"
  | "e" -> "E"
  | "f" -> "F"
  | "g" -> "G"
  | "h" -> "H"
  | "i" -> "I"
  | "j" -> "J"
  | "k" -> "K"
  | "l" -> "L"
  | "m" -> "M"
  | "n" -> "N"
  | "o" -> "O"
  | "p" -> "P"
  | "q" -> "Q"
  | "r" -> "R"
  | "s" -> "S"
  | "t" -> "T"
  | "u" -> "U"
  | "v" -> "V"
  | "w" -> "W"
  | "x" -> "X"
  | "y" -> "Y"
  | "z" -> "Z"
  | _ -> raise Not_found
end;

  | "a" -> "A"
  | "b" -> "B"
  | "c" -> "C"
  | "d" -> "D"
  | "e" -> "E"
  | "f" -> "F"
  | "g" -> "G"
  | "h" -> "H"
  | "i" -> "I"
  | "j" -> "J"
  | "k" -> "K"
  | "l" -> "L"
  | "m" -> "M"
  | "n" -> "N"
  | "o" -> "O"
  | "p" -> "P"
  | "q" -> "Q"
  | "r" -> "R"
  | "s" -> "S"
  | "t" -> "T"
  | "u" -> "U"
  | "v" -> "V"
  | "w" -> "W"
  | "x" -> "X"
  | "y" -> "Y"
  | "z" -> "Z"
  | _ -> raise Not_found
end;
